msg:Taking advantage of the May Day holiday to take the children out for a walk, at the request of my daughter, the hotel requires a bathtub and a tent. For a family with two children, the bed must be big enough. After choosing for a long time, I feel that only Fulitai International Hotel meets the requirements and the price is reasonable. We arrived at 10 o'clock on the day of check-in. I thought we would have to wait until 2 o'clock to check in, but I didn't expect Niu Xueping and Liu Yanhui at the front desk to check us in enthusiastically and upgrade us to a big-mouthed monkey theme room for free.
As soon as we entered the guest room, Xiaoqing from the housekeeping depar**ent brought fruits and yogurt in time. Because there were more of us and the water consumption was relatively large, Xiaohong and Xiaona from the housekeeping depar**ent brought us mineral water and quilts, which was really meticulous care.
Breakfast was what the two little ghosts looked forward to the most. I met the enthusiastic aunt Wang Li again, who kept helping the children get things and also took my favorite American for me.
When the children were reluctant to check out, they said that they would stay in this hotel next time they come to Yantai. Just when they were about to leave, they received a gift from Uncle Li Xiaocheng. It was such a surprise. The children were very happy and said that they would give this hotel 120 points.
After staying in so many hotels, this hotel really impressed us. This is a warm hotel with just the right service temperature. Thanks to Niu Xueqing, Liu Yanhui, Xiaoqing, Xiaohong, Xiaona, Wang Li, and Li Xiaocheng for bringing the children wonderful memories.
